                                    155 *                                                                       00154000
                                    156 * NOTES -                                                               00155000
                                    157 *        1. THIS MODULE MUST START ON A PAGE BOUNDARY.                  00156000
                                    158 *        2. THIS MODULE CANNOT EXCEED A FULL PAGE IN SIZE.              00157000

                                    171 *                                                                       00170000
                                    172 *        THIS FCB MACRO IS USED TO CREATE A 3211 OR 3203                00171000
                                    173 *        FORMS CONTROL BUFFER LOAD IMAGE.                               00172000
                                    174 *                                                                       00173000
                                    175 *                                                                       00174000
                                    176 *        +----+-----+-------------------------------------------------+ 00175000
                                    177 *        |    | FCB | FCB-NAME,SPACING,LENGTH,(LINE,CHANNEL,...),INDEX| 00176000
                                    178 *        +----+-----+-------------------------------------------------+ 00177000
                                    179 *                                                                       00178000
                                    180 *                                                                       00179000
                                    181 * FCB-NAME -                                                            00180000
                                    182 *                                                                       00181000
                                    183 *        ONE TO FOUR ALPHABETIC AND/OR NUMERIC CHARACTER NAME           00182000
                                    184 *        TO BE ASSIGNED TO THE BUFFER LOAD IMAGE.                       00183000
                                    185 *                                                                       00184000
                                    186 *        EXAMPLES -           A11,1234,WXYZ,A,L                         00185000
                                    187 *                                                                       00186000
                                    188 *                                                                       00187000
                                    189 * SPACING -                                                             00188000
                                    190 *                                                                       00189000
                                    191 *        CARRIAGE SPACING - ENTER 6 FOR SIX LINES PER INCH              00190000
                                    192 *        OR 8 FOR EIGHT LINES PER INCH. DEFAULT IS 6 LINES              00191000
                                    193 *        PER INCH.  IF THIS OPERAND IS OMITTED, COMMA                   00192000
                                    194 *        MUST BE PRESENT.                                               00193000
                                    195 *                                                                       00194000
                                    196 *                                                                       00195000
                                    197 * LENGTH -                                                              00196000
                                    198 *                                                                       00197000
                                    199 *        ENTER NUMBER (1 TO 180) OF PRINT LINES PER PAGE OR             00198000
                                    200 *        CARRIAGE TAPE.                                                 00199000
                                    201 *                                                                       00200000
                                    202 *                                                                       00201000
                                    203 * (LINE,CHANNEL,....)                                                   00202000
                                    204 *                                                                       00203000
                                    205 *        ENTER PRINT (LINE) NUMBER (1 TO THE VALUE OF LENGTH) AND       00204000
                                    206 *        (CHANNEL) VALUE (1 TO 12) FOR THAT PRINT LINE.                 00205000
                                    207 *                                                                       00206000
                                    208 *        EXAMPLE -                                                      00207000
                                    209 *              (3,1,60,12)                                              00208000
                                    210 *                             PRINT LINE 3 CHANNEL 1                    00209000
                                    211 *                             PRINT LINE 60 CHANNEL 12                  00210000
                                    212 *                                                                       00211000
                                    213 *                                                                       00212000
                                    214 * INDEX -                                                               00213000
                                    215 *                                                                       00214000
                                    216 *        ENTER 1 TO 31.  THE VALUE IS THE NUMBER OF THE PRINT POSITION  00215000
                                    217 *        THAT IS THE FIRST PRINTED POSITION.                            00216000
                                    218 *                                                                       00217000
                                    219 *        EXAMPLE -                                                      00218000

                                      3 *.                                                                      00003000
                                      4 * MODULE NAME -                                                         00004000
                                      5 *        DMKSNT                                                         00005000
                                      6 *                                                                       00006000
                                      7 * FUNCTION -                                                            00007000
                                      8 *                                                                       00008000
                                      9 *        THIS MODULE WILL BE ASSEMBLED BY THE INSTALLATION SYSTEM       00009000
                                     10 *        PROGRAMMER. IT WILL DESCRIBE THE THE SYSTEM TO BE SAVED VIA    00010000
                                     11 *        THE 'SAVESYS' COMMAND AND TO BE IPL'ED BY NAME. SHARED SEG-    00011000
                                     12 *        MENTS MAY BE SPECIFIED. THESE SEGMENTS MUST CONSIST OF         00012000
                                     13 *        ALL REENTRANT CODE.                                            00013000
                                     14 *                                                                       00014000
                                     15 *                                                                       00015000
                                     16 *        INPUT TO THE NAMESYS MACRO IS SPECIFIED IN THE FOLLOWING       00016000
                                     17 *        FORMAT:                                                        00017000
                                     18 *                                                                       00018000
                                     19 *        LABEL NAMESYS    SYSSIZE=NNNK,SYSNAME=CCCCCC,VSYSRES=CCCCCC,   00019000
                                     20 *                         VSYSADR=XXX,SYSVOL=CCCCCC,SYSCYL=NNN,         00020000
                                     21 *                         SYSSTRT=(CC,P),SYSPGCT=NN,                    00021000
                                     22 *                         SYSPGNM=(NN,NN,NN-NN,......),                 00022000
                                     23 *                         SYSHRSG=(N,N,...)                             00023000
                                     24 *                                                                       00024000
                                     25 *        WHERE:                                                         00025000
                                     26 *                                                                       00026000
                                     27 *        SYSSIZE - THIS IS THE MINUMUM STORAGE SIZE NEEDED TO           00027000
                                     28 *                  OPERATE THE SAVED SYSTEM.                            00028000
                                     29 *        SYSNAME - IS THE NAME GIVEN THE SYSTEM TO BE USED FOR          00029000
                                     30 *                  IDENTIFICATION BY 'SAVESYS' AND 'IPL'.               00030000
                                     31 *        VSYSRES - IS THE VOLUME SERIAL OF THE DASD CONTAINING THE      00031000
                                     32 *                  SYSTEM TO BE SAVED                                   00032000
                                     33 *        VSYSADR - IS THE VIRTUAL ADDRESS OF THE DASD CONTAINING        00033000
                                     34 *                  THE SYSTEM.                                          00034000
                                     35 *        SYSCYL  - THE CYLINDER ADDRESS OF THE 'MINI-DISK'              00035000
                                     36 *                  FOR THE SYSTEM TO BE SAVED.                          00036000
                                     37 *        SYSVOL  - IS THE VOLUME SERIAL OF THE DASD DESIGNATED TO       00037000
                                     38 *                  RECEIVE THE SAVED SYSTEM. THIS MUST BE A             00038000
                                     39 *                 'CP-OWNED' VOLUME.                                    00039000
                                     40 *        SYSSTRT - THIS DESIGNATES THE STARTING CYLINDER AND PAGE       00040000
                                     41 *                  ADDRESS ON 'SYSVOL' THAT THIS NAMED SYSTEM IS TO     00041000
                                     42 *                  BE SAVED. DURING THE SAVESYS AND IPL PROCESSING,     00042000
                                     43 *                  THIS WILL BE USED TO MAKE UP THE 'CCPD' ADDRESS      00043000
                                     44 *                  FOR THE DASD OPERATIONS. THESE NUMBERS ARE TO        00044000
                                     45 *                  SPECIFIED IN DECIMAL.                                00045000
                                     46 *        SYSPGCT - IS THE TOTAL NUMBER OF PAGES TO BE SAVED.            00046000
                                     47 *        SYSPGNM - THESE ARE THE NUMBERS OF THE PAGES TO BE SAVED.      00047000
                                     48 *                  SPECIFICATION MAY BE DONE AS GROUPS OF PAGES OR      00048000
                                     49 *                  AS SINGLE PAGES. FOR EXAMPLE - IF PAGES 0,4, AND     00049000
                                     50 *                  10 THRU 13 ARE TO BE SAVED, USE THE FORMAT:          00050000
                                     51 *                  SYSPGNM=(0,4,10-13).                                 00051000
                                     52 *        SYSHRSG - THESE ARE THE SEGMENT NUMBERS DESIGNATED AS          00052000
                                     53 *                  SHARED. THE PAGES IN THESE SEGMENTS WILL BE SET      00053000
                                     54 *                  UP AT IPL TIME TO BE USED BE ANY USER                00054000
                                     55 *                  IPL'ING BY THIS NAME.                                00055000
